# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy xDS Aggregated Discovery Service Server

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) gRPC server: the gRPC stream handler, the resource subscription tracking, the delta-xDS state machine, and the ACK/NACK processing.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)

- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Envoy ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) gRPC server implementation. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **27 C++ source files** in envoyproxy/envoy (v1.31.2) that implement the ADS gRPC server. These are organized into several key components:

### Core Components:

1. **Stream Handler & Muxer** - GrpcMuxImpl hierarchy managing the gRPC stream and resource multiplexing
2. **gRPC Stream Management** - GrpcStream, GrpcStreamInterface, and failover support
3. **Delta-xDS State Machine** - DeltaSubscriptionState with resource state tracking
4. **SotW xDS State Machine** - SotwSubscriptionState for state-of-the-world protocol
5. **Resource Tracking** - WatchMap managing subscription watches and callbacks
6. **ACK/NACK Processing** - PausableAckQueue and error detail handling
7. **Subscription Factories** - Factory classes for creating subscription types

### Key Processing Flow:

The implementation follows this pattern:
- gRPC receives DiscoveryResponse/DeltaDiscoveryResponse
- GrpcStream::onReceiveMessage() forwards to callbacks
- Subscription state machines process responses
- Resources are extracted and cached
- WatchMap notifies interested subsystems (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS, etc.)
- ACKs/NACKs are queued with response nonces and error details

The answer file at `/workspace/answer.json` contains the complete file listing, key symbols, the processing chain, and a detailed narrative explanation of the architecture and protocol flow.

Main ADS Stream Handler and Muxer\\nThe primary gRPC stream handler is implemented in the GrpcMuxImpl class hierarchy:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc**: Template-based GrpcMuxImpl class that manages subscriptions and handles both SotW and Delta variants via template specialization. Creates GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta concrete implementations.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc**: NewGrpcMuxImpl specifically handles delta-xDS on the unified gRPC stream.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h**: Legacy GrpcMuxImpl for handling discovery requests and responses.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/null_grpc_mux_impl.h**: Null implementation when ADS is not configured.\\n\\n### 2. gRPC Stream Management\\nActual gRPC stream handling is implemented via:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h**: Template-based GrpcStream class implementing GrpcStreamInterface, handles AsyncStreamCallbacks from gRPC client, manages reconnection, and forwards messages to GrpcStreamCallbacks.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream_interface.h**: Abstract interface defining GrpcStream contract.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: GrpcMuxFailover template class that manages primary and failover stream switching.\\n\\n### 3. Delta-xDS State Machine\\nThe incremental xDS protocol state is managed by:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Core delta-xDS state machine tracking resource subscriptions, wildcard subscriptions, and ambiguous resources. Implements updateSubscriptionInterest(), getNextRequest(), handleGoodResponse(), handleBadResponse() for ACK/NACK processing, and addResourceStateFromServer() for processing server resource updates.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy version of delta subscription state (deprecated in favor of xds_mux version).\\n\\nThe ResourceState nested class tracks whether each resource is in \\\"waitingForServer\\\", \\\"complete\\\", or has a specific version. It maintains three maps: requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_ to handle the complex state transitions of the delta protocol.\\n\\n### 4. State-of-the-World (SotW) xDS State Machine\\nThe SotW protocol state is managed by:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: SotwSubscriptionState class implementing BaseSubscriptionState template, tracking subscribed resources and their versions. Generates full DiscoveryRequests with all subscribed resource names and handles version tracking.\\n\\n### 5. Base Subscription State\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h**: BaseSubscriptionState template class providing common interface for both SotW and Delta variants. Implements response handling flow via handleResponse(), calling handleGoodResponse() for success or handleBadResponse() for exceptions.\\n\\n### 6. Resource Watch/Subscription Tracking\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: WatchMap class implementing SubscriptionCallbacks interface. Manages watches for resource subscriptions, tracks which resources are requested by which watchers, and notifies watchers of configuration updates via onConfigUpdate() callbacks.\\n\\n### 7. Subscription Implementation\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: GrpcSubscriptionImpl and GrpcCollectionSubscriptionImpl classes implementing Subscription interface. Connect individual subsystem subscriptions (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS, etc.) to the shared GrpcMux.\\n\\n### 8. ACK/NACK Queue Management\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: PausableAckQueue managing acknowledgment queuing and pausing/resuming. Coordinates with GrpcMux for rate-limited ACK delivery. Implements UpdateAck structure for nonce tracking and error_detail population for NACKs.\\n\\n### 9. Configuration and Context\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: GrpcMuxContext struct containing parameters needed for GrpcMux creation: async_client, local_info, dispatcher, stats, rate_limit_settings.\\n\\n### 10. Subscription Factories\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Factory classes including GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory for creating appropriate subscription types.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Factory for collection-based subscriptions including AdsCollectionConfigSubscriptionFactory.\\n\\n## Protocol Processing Flow:\\n\\nWhen the gRPC stream receives a DiscoveryResponse/DeltaDiscoveryResponse:\\n1. **GrpcStream::onReceiveMessage()** forwards to **GrpcStreamCallbacks::onDiscoveryResponse()**\\n2. **GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse()** routes to subscription-specific handler\\n3. **DeltaSubscriptionState::handleResponse()** or **SotwSubscriptionState::handleResponse()** processes the response\\n4. **handleGoodResponse()** extracts and processes resources, updating ResourceState via addResourceStateFromServer()\\n5. **handleBadResponse()** populates error_detail for NACK scenarios\\n6. **WatchMap::onConfigUpdate()** notifies all interested watches/callbacks\\n7. **getNextRequest()** prepares ACK with response_nonce for next DeltaDiscoveryRequest\\n8. **PausableAckQueue** manages rate-limited transmission of ACKs\\n\\nThe implementation supports both aggregated (ADS) and non-aggregated xDS variants, delta-xDS and SotW xDS protocols, and failover to secondary control plane servers.\"\n}\n",

Main ADS Stream Handler and Muxer\\nThe primary gRPC stream handler is implemented in the GrpcMuxImpl class hierarchy:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc**: Template-based GrpcMuxImpl class that manages subscriptions and handles both SotW and Delta variants via template specialization. Creates GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta concrete implementations.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc**: NewGrpcMuxImpl specifically handles delta-xDS on the unified gRPC stream.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h**: Legacy GrpcMuxImpl for handling discovery requests and responses.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/null_grpc_mux_impl.h**: Null implementation when ADS is not configured.\\n\\n### 2. gRPC Stream Management\\nActual gRPC stream handling is implemented via:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h**: Template-based GrpcStream class implementing GrpcStreamInterface, handles AsyncStreamCallbacks from gRPC client, manages reconnection, and forwards messages to GrpcStreamCallbacks.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream_interface.h**: Abstract interface defining GrpcStream contract.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: GrpcMuxFailover template class that manages primary and failover stream switching.\\n\\n### 3. Delta-xDS State Machine\\nThe incremental xDS protocol state is managed by:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Core delta-xDS state machine tracking resource subscriptions, wildcard subscriptions, and ambiguous resources. Implements updateSubscriptionInterest(), getNextRequest(), handleGoodResponse(), handleBadResponse() for ACK/NACK processing, and addResourceStateFromServer() for processing server resource updates.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy version of delta subscription state (deprecated in favor of xds_mux version).\\n\\nThe ResourceState nested class tracks whether each resource is in \\\"waitingForServer\\\", \\\"complete\\\", or has a specific version. It maintains three maps: requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_ to handle the complex state transitions of the delta protocol.\\n\\n### 4. State-of-the-World (SotW) xDS State Machine\\nThe SotW protocol state is managed by:\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: SotwSubscriptionState class implementing BaseSubscriptionState template, tracking subscribed resources and their versions. Generates full DiscoveryRequests with all subscribed resource names and handles version tracking.\\n\\n### 5. Base Subscription State\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h**: BaseSubscriptionState template class providing common interface for both SotW and Delta variants. Implements response handling flow via handleResponse(), calling handleGoodResponse() for success or handleBadResponse() for exceptions.\\n\\n### 6. Resource Watch/Subscription Tracking\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: WatchMap class implementing SubscriptionCallbacks interface. Manages watches for resource subscriptions, tracks which resources are requested by which watchers, and notifies watchers of configuration updates via onConfigUpdate() callbacks.\\n\\n### 7. Subscription Implementation\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: GrpcSubscriptionImpl and GrpcCollectionSubscriptionImpl classes implementing Subscription interface. Connect individual subsystem subscriptions (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS, etc.) to the shared GrpcMux.\\n\\n### 8. ACK/NACK Queue Management\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: PausableAckQueue managing acknowledgment queuing and pausing/resuming. Coordinates with GrpcMux for rate-limited ACK delivery. Implements UpdateAck structure for nonce tracking and error_detail population for NACKs.\\n\\n### 9. Configuration and Context\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: GrpcMuxContext struct containing parameters needed for GrpcMux creation: async_client, local_info, dispatcher, stats, rate_limit_settings.\\n\\n### 10. Subscription Factories\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Factory classes including GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory for creating appropriate subscription types.\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_collection_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Factory for collection-based subscriptions including AdsCollectionConfigSubscriptionFactory.\\n\\n## Protocol Processing Flow:\\n\\nWhen the gRPC stream receives a DiscoveryResponse/DeltaDiscoveryResponse:\\n1. **GrpcStream::onReceiveMessage()** forwards to **GrpcStreamCallbacks::onDiscoveryResponse()**\\n2. **GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse()** routes to subscription-specific handler\\n3. **DeltaSubscriptionState::handleResponse()** or **SotwSubscriptionState::handleResponse()** processes the response\\n4. **handleGoodResponse()** extracts and processes resources, updating ResourceState via addResourceStateFromServer()\\n5. **handleBadResponse()** populates error_detail for NACK scenarios\\n6. **WatchMap::onConfigUpdate()** notifies all interested watches/callbacks\\n7. **getNextRequest()** prepares ACK with response_nonce for next DeltaDiscoveryRequest\\n8. **PausableAckQueue** manages rate-limited transmission of ACKs\\n\\nThe implementation supports both aggregated (ADS) and non-aggregated xDS variants, delta-xDS and SotW xDS protocols, and failover to secondary control plane servers.\"\n}\n",
